21 #define GLITCHEDHTTPS_CA_CERTS (_glitchedhttps_get_ca_certs())
22 
23 /*
24  * This part of the work contains a (modified) version of Mozilla's "certdata.txt" file (see links below)
25  * as a provider of commonly trusted CA root certificates (the same ones that the Firefox browser uses).
26  *
27  *
28  * Additional custom picks for backup purposes (appended at the end of the above mentioned Mozilla chain; duplicate entries are possible)
29  * were taken from the following sources:
30  *
31  * +--------------------------+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
32  * | CERTIFICATE AUTHORITY | CERTIFICATES DOWNLOAD URL |
33  * +--------------------------+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
34  * | Let's Encrypt | https://letsencrypt.org/certificates/ |
35  * +--------------------------+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
36  * | DigiCert | https://www.digicert.com/digicert-root-community-certificates.htm |
37  * +--------------------------+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
38  * | SwissSign | https://www.swisssign.com/support/ca-prod.html |
39  * +--------------------------+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
40  * | SSL.com | https://www.ssl.com/article/ssl-com-root-certificates/ |
41  * +--------------------------+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
42  * | IdenTrust | https://www.identrust.com/support/downloads |
43  * +--------------------------+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
44  * | VeriSign/Symantec | https://www.symantec.com/en/au/theme/roots |
45  * +--------------------------+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
46  * | Comodo | https://support.comodo.com/index.php?/Knowledgebase/List/Index/71 |
47  * +--------------------------+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
48  * | GoDaddy | https://ssl-ccp.godaddy.com/repository?origin=CALLISTO |
49  * +--------------------------+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
50  * | GlobalSign | https://support.globalsign.com/customer/portal/articles/1426602-globalsign-root-certificates |
51  * +--------------------------+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
52  * | Amazon Trust Services | https://www.amazontrust.com/repository/ |
53  * +--------------------------+------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
54  */
55 
57 static char* _glitchedhttps_ca_certs = NULL;
58 
59 /* NOTE:
60  * If this internal _glitchedhttps_get_ca_certs() function fails it returns a NULL or EMPTY string,
61  * which will most likely result in HTTPS requests failing due to untrusted SSL certificates!
62  */
63 
65 static char* _glitchedhttps_get_ca_certs()
66 {
67  if (_glitchedhttps_ca_certs != NULL)
68  {
69  return _glitchedhttps_ca_certs;
70  }
71 
72  FILE* file = fopen(__FILE__, "r");
73  if (file == NULL)
74  {
75  return "";
76  }
77 
78  chillbuff stringbuilder;
79  chillbuff_init(&stringbuilder, 320000, sizeof(char), CHILLBUFF_GROW_DUPLICATIVE);
80 
81  char buffer[256];
82  bool reading = false;
83 
84  while (fgets(buffer, sizeof buffer, file) != NULL)
85  {
86  if (strncmp(buffer, "-----BEGIN CERTIFICATES LIST-----", 33) == 0)
87  {
88  reading = true;
89  }
90 
91  if (reading)
92  {
93  chillbuff_push_back(&stringbuilder, buffer, strlen(buffer));
94  }
95 
96  if (strncmp(buffer, "-----END CERTIFICATES LIST-----", 31) == 0)
97  {
98  reading = false;
99  }
100  }
101 
102  _glitchedhttps_ca_certs = malloc(stringbuilder.length + 1);
103  if (_glitchedhttps_ca_certs == NULL)
104  {
105  goto exit;
106  }
107 
108  memcpy((char*)_glitchedhttps_ca_certs, (char*)stringbuilder.array, stringbuilder.length);
109  _glitchedhttps_ca_certs[stringbuilder.length] = '\0';
110 
111 exit:
112  chillbuff_free(&stringbuilder);
113  fclose(file);
114 
115  return _glitchedhttps_ca_certs;
116 }
117 
118 /*
119  ##
120  ## Bundle of CA Root Certificates
121  ##
122  ## Certificate data from Mozilla as of: Wed Nov 27 04:12:10 2019 GMT
123  ##
124  ## This is a bundle of X.509 certificates of public Certificate Authorities
125  ## (CA). These were automatically extracted from Mozilla's root certificates
126  ## file (certdata.txt). This file can be found in the mozilla source tree:
127  ## https://hg.mozilla.org/releases/mozilla-release/raw-file/default/security/nss/lib/ckfw/builtins/certdata.txt
128  ##
129  ## It contains the certificates in PEM format and therefore
130  ## can be directly used with curl / libcurl / php_curl, or with
131  ## an Apache+mod_ssl webserver for SSL client authentication.
132  ## Just configure this file as the SSLCACertificateFile.
133  ##
134  ## Conversion done with mk-ca-bundle.pl version 1.27.
135  ## SHA256: 607309057d0ec70f8e4e97b03906bafb2fcebb24cd37b5e8293e681ae26ceae0
136  ##
137 
138 
139  This modified variant of the Mozilla "certdata.txt" file was taken from the CURL website:
140 
141  https://curl.haxx.se/docs/caextract.html
142 
143  The original file, as well as infos regarding Mozilla's certificate handling approach can be found here:
144 
145  https://wiki.mozilla.org/CA/Included_Certificates
146 
147  https://wiki.mozilla.org/CA/Additional_Trust_Changes
148 
149  https://www.mozilla.org/en-US/about/governance/policies/security-group/certs/
150 
151  https://hg.mozilla.org/mozilla-central/raw-file/tip/security/nss/lib/ckfw/builtins/certdata.txt
152 
153  (Links last accessed successfully the 28th of December, 2019)
154 
155 */
